人民委員會之下。它不僅是蘇聯科學的參謀本部，而且是新社會建設的一個設計機關；有了它，不僅統一了全蘇聯的科學戰綫，集中了全國的科學者在建設新社會發展新文化新科學之下努力，而且使得科學戰綫與新社會建設緊密地聯繫在一起了。業餘修學梵娥玲學習初步  風　　請問，先生，為什麽在這個世界上，在同樣的吃飯穿衣的生活形式之下，會生出兩種不同的人來，一種樂於求生，非常快活，一種萎靡頹廢，懨懨欲死？　　理由很簡單：前一種是知道用旁的東西來調劑這吃飯穿衣呆板生活的人，而後一種則只見到吃飯穿衣的枯燥和累贅。　　生活，若單從吃飯穿衣一方面看，眞如一片大沙漢，尤其是負了家庭生活責任的人，一天只感到忙碌，苦悶，壓迫……！可是，若果我們在繁忙之餘能有自己歡喜的東西來換換胃口，則一天的困倦與煩愁便都會忘記得乾乾淨淨，因而不覺其生活之苦的。　　調劑枯燥生活最好的東西决不是又麻雀，也不是逛跳舞塲，我以為最好的，莫如自己抽空學一點音樂，而音樂當中最容易使人陶醉的，那便是梵娥玲（Siolin）了！　　梵娥玲有「音樂皇后」之稱，第一是指牠的音色比一切樂器的都要豐富美麗，第二是說牠艱難不易學好。說到牠的音色之豐富和美麗，那是不容諱言的了；至於說牠艱難不易學，則現在已有許多人加以否認，我也以為只要歡喜牠，用點心思，勤於練習，是沒有學不好的。　　梵娥玲有些像把圓形肚子改成為葫蘆形肚子的中國月琴；有一個螺絲形的捲曲的頭，頭兩旁各有兩個絞絃的柱約長二寸半，頭下是約五寸長的一根細細的頸，頸下是一個約一尺二三寸長的葫蘆形肚子，從頭到肚子的末端，共計長約一尺七八寸（孩子梵娥玲較短小）。這小小的樂器，形式非常美麗可愛，各部份有各部份的特殊名稱：頭和頸便呌頭與頸，頸以下的肚皮，名字可就多了，這肚皮是一個篇形的木盒子，背上的板呌背板，前面的板呌腹板，腹板上在葫蘆灣腰的地方，一邊開了一個嬾嬾的子形的孔，這孔呌做子孔，在整個樂器的音色之「好」與「不好」上是有頂大頂大的關係的。盒子裏面，在右邊子孔的左下方，有一根小小的木棒，撐着背板與腹板，是作由腹板而到背板，傳達聲音，使全個肚皮的每一部份都起共鳴作用之用的，這呌做昔柱。此外還有一條一半膠在頸上，一半空虛在腹板上，長約七八寸，上窄下寬的木板，呌做墊弦板，這，顧名思義，便知是作為墊弦用的。弦從頭上的弦柱旋住一端，牽過道板，扣在一塊摺扇形的本板上，道本板再以旁的粗弦扣在梵娥玲的背板末端上。在弦經過背板時，再用一小片未染而彫鐫很美的木片架在兩子孔的中央，這白色的木片呌馬或橋。　　梵娥玲通身是咖啡色的，惟弦柱，墊弦板及扇形木是黑的，馬是白的，所以全部的色彩異常調和。　　梵娥玲的全身都係木製，但不是普通的粗木，是紋理非常細緻，組織非常緊密的一種特殊木材做的。木身的表面上有一層金光閃閃的漆；據說這漆於樂器的優劣上也有極大的關係，在古代有一個專漆梵娥玲的意大利人，經他漆出的，音聲格外美好，但可惜這方法至今已失傳了。買梵娥玲的人必須先砍背板與腹板平直與否，然後再看那上面的紋理紊不紊亂，最後才口表面的漆均不均勻，這三點是很要法意的。梵娥玲除了這個身體以外，還有一隻長約三尺的弓，弓桿稍彎；弓末有一寸餘的柄，從柄到弓梢有一片白色的馬尾；這便是用來摩擦琴弦而發聲的。這馬尾可以由弓柄旋緊或放鬆，依拉琴時的需要而決定。　　知道了梵娥玲的構造以後，便要談到初步學習的方法了。　　梵娥玲上有四條弦，一端捲在弦柱上，一端經過馬而扣在扇形木上。這四條所發出來的聲音相當於鋼琴上的·3，6，2，5·所以呌發香為·3的做E弦，6的做A玆，2的做D弦，5·的做G弦。在五線譜上E弦的音符在第四間，A弦的音符在第二間，D弦的音符在下加第一間，G弦的音符在下加第三簡。這四個音和各音符的位置必須記牢，然後在拉琴時，其他的音依次類推起來才比較的迅速。　　拉琴的時候，第一須法意的是托琴，執弓及站立的姿勢。將琴的腹部擱在左肩上，用左腮夾緊，不使搖落，再用左手虎口托着琴頸，四指在內，曲屈以按琴弦，大拇指在外，以助托琴時的力量。左手不可緊握琴頸，須使能在琴頸上來去自如；左手臂略與琴身平行，左手掌及四指與琴頸略成直角。左手托定琴後，右手則拿起弓來，用大拇指及四指拈緊弓柄，大拇指貼在黏馬尾的拐灣處，其他四指則並列在弓柄上，但只用指尖，切勿使弓柄擱入手指的第二節或第二節以上。　　兩隻手都安排定了，然後端端正正站在琴譜的前面；琴譜的位置須與眼一樣高：眼正視，頭勿高抬，也勿下俛。再，右手舉起來，將弓的馬尾放在馬的前邊，卽在墊弦板末端與馬之間的地方，從弓末到弓梢，一弓一弓的慢慢拉起來；弓與弦成正十字形，不得偏斜；弓上上下時，右手手指不能隨　　初學習時，左手托定琴頸，勿動，右手用力，一根弦，一根弦的慢慢的拉，使發出來的聲音不像雞呌或猪呌才對。先拉G弦，上下往返至少二十回，再拉D弦，以次才拉A弦和E弦。　　不按弦而拉的音符，琴譜上往往在那音符的頂端畫一小圓圈，英文呌Open　String。練習Open　String是梵娥玲初步學習最重要的功夫，這一步功夫若不成熟，底下是難得學好的。　　用弓的方法也是極其重要的，每個音符有每種弓法，初學者的琴譜上已經明白註出來了，拉時必須按照其方法。在譜上寫出　符號的，表示這音符須用下弓（Donwn　Bow），所謂下弓者即是由弓尾起到弓梢止，註有V的為上弓（Up　Bow），與下弓相反，由弓梢起到弓尾止。還有只需要用半弓的，琴譜上也註明Half　Bow，用整弓的，註明Whale　Row；若幾個音連在一起只用一弓或半弓的，則這幾個音以一綫括起來，如1356，四音只用一弓。　　梵娥玲的弓法複雜得很，不過這幾種是初學者必須知道的罷了。　　此外，左手指的按法也有一定，該用那一個手指的，一定要依照譜上註出的規定，切不可自由更動。譜上註有1，2，3，4的地方，便是指定你必須用那一個手指。前面已經說過，左手的大拇指是不按弦的，因此譜上的一是指左手的食指，2她指中指，3是指無名指，4是指小指。按弦時須用指尖，並須用力，如此則發出的聲音才沉着，宏亮，而不致浮滑或枯燥乏味了。　　拉琴的第一要着，是聲音要正，拍子要準；聲音正靠聽覺，多聽音樂的人，一絲一亳的聲的差誤都是分辨得出來的。但初學的人可以以多練習及用音笛或鋼琴來矯正。至於拍子，初學習時可用右脚在地上輕輕拍擊，久了，不用脚拍，心裏耳裏也自有一定的節奏了。拍擊時，初起總以慢為佳，普通用一拍的，這時可以以四拍的時間來代替，這不但可以使拍子準確，便是這長長的一弓也可以使右腕的力量因訓練而逐漸加强了。　　前面說過，梵娥玲的四條弦為E，A，D，G。那末，要是沒有鋼琴對音的時候怎麽辦呢？買梵娥玲時可以順便買一音笛或音又。音笛有四管，即是E，A，D，G四音，是專門預備給梵娥玲對音用的；用時非常便當，用口吹某管，以右手轉某弦，左手拇指撥弦作聲，到弦聲與笛音相合為止。音又音為6，與A同，對音時，將音又在桌上用力一擊，趕快將又柄立在梵娥玲的腹板上，即聽見嗡然的悠長之聲，　這時速撥A弦，使與這嗡聲相合。A弦調準後，再調E，再調D和G。因為G到D，D到A，A到E都是全五度，有了一個標準，其他的音調起來是很容易的。　　梵娥玲練習完畢，須將各弦及馬尾放鬆，這是保護樂器的唯一良法。千萬別以對音麻煩而不放鬆，不然，恐下次練習時，弦也斷了，馬尾也失了緊張力，而換起弦來還更加麻煩。　　無論學習什麽都需要勤于練習，但有了固定職業的人，不能將整日的功夫都貢獻給為了調劑生活的一種樂器，那可怎麽辦呢？其實，每日有一小時的練習己很夠了，可是不能間斷，一曝十寒是絕對造不出成績來的。　　生活眞似一片大沙澳，只有音樂才是這沙漢上的一泓清泉！在一天繁重的工作之後，肩着琴，對着斜暉，拉一二曲輕婉曼妙的短歌，不用訴說，這個個珠圓顫動的音巳將你一生的辛苦吐給淸風，傳給大地了！熱烈悲壯的「馬賽曲」，是一位小軍官在一個革命會議之後，用梵娥玲隨意拉出來的，他當時革命的熱情便幻成了燦爛的自由之花，開遍了法蘭西，蔓延了全世界！　　神秘的音樂，美妙的梵娥玲，願你去救每個人精神上的饑渴呵！　　以下接第五版旅行一周普陀拜石聽潮記  守愚　　在初秋曼妙的微風中，為了考查漁業，跟了幾個友人乘了輪船，在江浙沿海去巡迥了一週。到了定海以後，再赴沈家門，因久聞普陀名勝，便往普陀去遊了一個暢快。　　普陀屬浙江定海，離寗波數百里，其間亦有小輪來往其間，均於黎明起程，傍晚時始抵普陀。此等商輪，其主要目的在於鎮海，舟山，沈家門等島上貿易，自甬埠至香陀須經三次停泊，每次又須等候上下貨物的半小時之久。如果由上海去，則夏秋之際，上海輪新江天及寗興等，每逢星期六下午四時由申起椗，次晨到甬，即放特班至香陀。又有舟山，穿山，大華，益利等數輪，每於六七月間行駛上，普間每週二次。陸路則可由杭州搭火車至寗波，再由奪波乘小火輪前往。總之，欲往香陀，寗波實為必經之地。當輪船一到普陀，便停泊在中流，那時就擁上來無數小帆船，爭先恐後的來搶擺渡生意。渡費單身者的一角，如行李多的，有索至國幣二元者。目前，因導游團體如中國旅行社及其他各種社團自己的臨時組織甚多，故已預有準備，使秩序井然。那時，各寺廟所派之接客員亦在上岸處鴣候，遊客可隨意選擇所欲住宿之寺廟，決定後，即可將行李交付該寺接客員，自己則任意步行或乘肩輿從容逛山。　　從輪船中遠望，見普陀孤峙海中，蜿蜒綿亘。據地理所載，該地縱橫各十餘里，周圍四十餘里，東按日本，北接登萊，南亙閩夸，西通吳越，實東海中一屏障。其最高處為白華頂，佛頂山，錦屏山，大小雪浪山，及光熙，象王，梅岑，達摩，正趣諸峯。東盡靑鼓聶，西盡風洞嘴，南盡道頭楊梅跳，北盡伏龍山等四境。小洛迦山峙其東南；翁洲諸山環其西北；月奧拱其南；霍山映其東北，此四望之景也。水之概，南深而北淺；山之分則東多而西少。外多平崗幽洞，內多崇岩曲澗。在諸浙名勝中普陀與杭州西湖，溫州雁蕩，嚴州富春江，天台石梁等齋名。如果把它和人們常去的西湖比較，則西湖四山合沓，水光清秀，林本葱籠，遠望如倩裝美人，婀娜嫵媚，令人悠然神柱；，普陀四面環海，山不甚高，無層崖複壁之觀，而奇險詭幻，洞壑大然，遠望之如披甲英雄，剛健勁　，令人肅然起敬。此不同之點也。普陀之最足動人者，則為各種石形之奇特，係他處所無。據我所經歷的遊程，可分為前山後山兩路。前山勝蹟較多，而山不甚高，雖婦人女子，亦可緩步遨遊，探奇尋幽，覽之不窮。後山荒蕪未闢，石徑峙嶇，峻峭難行。風景亦不如前山之佳，惟慧濟寺及梵音洞古佛洞諸名勝而已。如不耐步行，可乘藤製山轎往，以免跋涉之苦。還有一座洛迦山，須在香陀之短姑道頭趁渡船往。距普陀西南僅十餘里，但水勢湍急，駕船不易，往往要幾小時才能到達。而船在行駛時顛簸甚劇，常令人嘔吐淋漓，故僧衆勸遊客枵腹而往，蓋恐飽食易嘔吐也。惟該處層巒疊嶂，洪波巨浸，盪浴日星，吐納烟霞，奇石嵯峨，崛出其間，頗足為名山生色。故普陀又有「補怛洛迦山」之稱。又普陀古有所謂十一勝景者，即（一）矮姑聖蹟，（二）兩洞潮聲，（三）千步金沙，（四）華頂雲濤，（五）光熙雪齊，（六）梅岑仙井，（七）法華靈洞，（八）潮陽湧日，（九）寳塔鬧鐘，（十）磐陀夕照，（十一）蓮池夜月，（十二）洛迦勝景。　　普陀有兩個特異於其他名勝之點：一便是「奇石」遍野；一便是「怒濤」澎湃。遊人得趣也多半因為這兩點。尤其是在秋高氣爽時，洶湧的在濤更是為愛好者極視聽之娛。據說普陀聽潮之處，第一要算潮音洞了。這洞在寺左龍灣之麓，金沙盡處，岩石叢起沙中，有畝餘廣闊，齒齒不能容足。從崖至洞脚，高二十丈，歧處如門，穹上虛下，官若漏屋。當潮水遇風在號，駛奔入洞，聲音便鏗訇鐺磕，聲如轟雷。洞巔有穴孔，名天窗，倒窺之玲瓏嵌掛，險怪百出，海濤吞吐，盈縮倐忽，每一浪投孔中，扼束上騰，飛洙噴沬，飄然從數十丈下，鬃鬆洒面，忽然便覺人身已沾濡了。目潮音之奇，不止洞內，洞口石門數處，巉岩佶屈，怒濤排突，若怒若嬸，令觀者眩目震耳，懾魄墮魂，嘆為觀止。第二處要算梵音洞，地在正東境，面大洋東去，土窮山盡，亦不知彼岸何處矣。斗然峭壁危峻，石色靑黑，高三四十丈，陡劈兩崖如門，洞深廣百餘丈，海潮人洞，激蕩有聲，如龍虎咆哮，雷霆怒興，聽者悚慄。因其繼續不斷，遠聽恍如蕭寺木魚，「可……可」不絕，故名「梵音」。與潮音洞東南相崎，如普陀靈壤之眉目然。第三為朝陽洞，在几寳嶺盡處（几寳嶺在東南境，山石落磊如珍寳委積茶几上，故名，俗稱饑飽，可笑）。複洞轉折，面臨東海，海濤時吼其下，勢如萬馬奔騰。在旭日初升時，奇景在望，氣象萬千，故名朝陽。千步沙即在其下飛沙奧附近（飛沙奧，在梵音洞主山靑鼓磊西八仙岩左近。其地皆係虛沙，履之輒欲陷，自東至西，亘三里，闊百餘丈。老僧相傳云，昔為淺海，後飛沙日積，漸成邱阜，高處至三五丈，而草木不生，曠寂可畏，但適茶山者，多取道於此）。自嶺至奧的五里長，循山稱玉堂街。沿海平沙一片，即為「千步」。每海潮拍岸，浪高數十丈，來如飛瀑，止如曳練，遇大汎激盪，則雷轟雪湧，爍目驚心，倏忽詭異，不可名狀。觀日觀潮之唯一處所，舍此莫屬。第四要算裭虎奧了，地在東北茶山盡處天竺山下，潮聲吼嘯，如哮虎然，故名。遊茶山者便道多往遊。茶山在白華頂高峯後，自北亘西，其地最廣，中多溪澗，山上產茶極富。寺僧於雨前採摘之以賽客，味極甘芳。山茶樹每高數丈，冬春之交丹花被谷，恍如珊瑚林。惟秋日無景可觀覽，以致　虎奧亦少遊人，故到者極少。其餘如南天門海濱，靑石灣，東北海中小山，珞伽山麓等地，亦常常怒濤　處，可觀可聽，惟無奇景異聲，可供玩味而巳。聽潮之餘，兼賞異石：如，磐陀石：：在山之西境，石支石上，狀如重台。下石周廣十丈，高身而尖頂，其則似磐陀之另一巨石託焉，其廣大於下石，旁空中倚，亦有　隙，窺之通明。據嚮導者云。用綫可以隔過。蓋二石本末相連云。然則何以能安如磐石，誠不可思議。石頂平坦，寬闊的十餘丈，可容百人，備短梯始能登其上，環眺山海，洋洋大觀。在磐陀石東，相離的百步，高若相望，傳係觀音大士說法處，故名說法台。在磐陀石西，又有所謂五十三參石，奇形石塊參差，轟立若聽講者，數目恐不甚合，不過相傳如此。又有二龜聽法石，亦在其西，一蹲石頂，一緣石直上，昂頭伸頸，筋脈盡露，可謂酷肖。此外又有柱空石，一石如柱，屹立空際。在白華山頂右之雪浪山，上多白石，朗朗然輝映林木，如積雪，又如湧浪，故名。其巔有八卦石，亂石排空，懸崖百伋，偃仰倚伏，突千元凹凸，西面又有巨石危懸石頂，搖之能動，而不下墮。又有馬鞍石，形如馬鞍。在西茶山上，又有雲法石，兩石下如欹錘，上如素碁，峻險奇特，危而不墮，上石有題字曰雲法，下石題字曰海天佛國。西南頻海之金剛峯側，有巫山石，意狀其高。怪石嵯峨，劈一為兩，似為巨靈五丁所變幻。在西天門右，有不二石，兩石相去丈許，稍參差前後而形模宛似，故曰不二，高廣各丈餘，如析珪剖璧之雙胞胎狀。不二石南崗，有平石廣畝許，與蘇州虎邱石相類，其大可坐千人。中載一石，形似菱角，橫陳一端，遠望之宛然一扁舟。磐陀石東，梅岑山腰，有石浪岩，高三十丈，石紋如浪，視之欲動。其側有巨石參差對列如門，高十餘丈，形如仙掌，昔人題曰天設閑關。西天門北，有圓通岩，大石險峻桀敖，或凌空孤峙，參差排突，循行環眺，無不隔閡，故名圓通。其後有石如鼎，名香一爐石。寺後之西巫山石下，有佛牙石，高的一丈，半凹半突如倒牙，又如樸頭，旁有異石，非洞非門，其形甚怪。在觀音洞側，有羈哥石，白石辣竚，圓首細頸而短身，其形酷肖羈哥，不類別鳥，誠奇觀也。摩尼洞西有天　石，形如簸箕飛沙奧西，功德嶺東盡處，陂陁間有石橫鋪三四十丈，平如恐突，色如水墨渲染，甚光油然，若展稍穀。與說法台租相望一石，名點頭石，高八丈，周廣約二十丈，孤峙平岩，旁懸中凑，憾之則動，若點頭然。在寺東，從觀音峯而下數百步，高五六丈，三面方廣如佛座，西稍窪狹，蓋觀音峯圓如側蓮，此石方如岸　也。西旁兩石，高不及半，一如掛衣，一如覆釡，皆斷崖懸　，不可登陟。遊人巨公，勒名其上，曰三一岩，又曰空有境，海天春曉，又有聯曰，寰區昭瑞相，剎海遍潮靑。又如佛手岩之疊子石，龍岩之蝦蟆石，屬歇庵之眞歇石，虎岩之靈芝石，葛洪井西之慈雲石，南天門崖石上之鼓石等，或以形象，或以古跡稱，均各有奇趣。至其餘山峯岩奧，則無甚出奇矣。

風俗誌不拉皮條拉衣帶　一杯咖啡訂終身　拉伯蘭人的特殊婚制  張企程　　拉伯蘭人（Laponoj）是居住瑞典北部的一種游牧民族，人口只有七千入。他們的言語和生活習慣都很特別，但是最使我們覺得特別的是他們的婚婚制度。他們還行着一種媒妁婚婚。這里我們就把他們的媒妁制度提出來講一講：　　在拉伯蘭人的社會里，一個年靑小伙子怎樣討一個老婆的風俗是各式各樣的，而同時也怪有趣的。最普通的是，當一個拉伯蘭男孩子成長為一個小伙子而需要一個女人的時候，他得先替自己找一個能夠去和他所愛的女子的父母開談判的媒人。第一步手續是他同着他的媒人一同去拜訪那位姑娘的帳幕（因為拉伯蘭人是都住在帳幕里的）。進了帳慕，與那家的主人互相敬禮問好以後，就一句話也不講地靜靜坐一些時候。於是那位靑年依了預先的定的辦法向媒人做一個暗號，那時媒人開始這樣說：「可允許我們在這里燒一點咖啡嗎？」「可以，可以，當然可以。誰都有權利在這里燒咖啡啊。」其時那位拉伯蘭靑年就從布袋里拿出燒咖啡的壺和杯子來，在壺里放滿了潔淨的雪（在那里終年不會斷雪），然後把它放在火上。水在火上燒，主客雙方就瞎七搭八地攀談起來，但是關於婚姻問題却絕口不談的。一面談，那靑年人就一面從布袋里拿出糖，乾乳酪同麵包來。咖啡一燒好，靑年自己先喝一杯，然後請男主人和女主人喝。倘然男女主人接受了他的咖啡，這就是說他們懂得了其中的道理，並且對議婚這件事完全同意。這里靑年人就可以進一步在男女主八同意之下請他們的女兒喝咖啡了。假使這位姑娘從靑年的手里接受了那杯咖啡，這就是表示她也愛着他。於是男女雙方就可以到附近的登記所去登記訂婚，而最後由牧師來完成結婚的儀式。　　也有靑年自己不到女子的家里去的，他只派他的媒人去。那媒人去打聽一下，間女家對於這議婚的事可有什麽反對之處。照例女家的父母要對男家的財產查問一下，問他有多少馴鹿（因為馴鹿可以說是拉伯蘭人唯一的產業），並且問一問他的品性怎樣。要是媒人所回答的都使他們滿意，就可以在女家的帳幕里開起訂婚的宴會來。未來的新郎以及男女雙方的親戚朋友都來參加宴會，每個親友都得帶一些物品（有時甚至是很貴重的東西）來，作為送給未婚夫婦的禮物。　　也有男子先向女子求愛，經女子同意後再央媒人去說親的。曾經有一次在一處大城市的市集里，一個男了碰倒了他所愛的一個女子。大家碰面之後，男子去拉一拉女子的衣帶。這是求愛的第一個表示。如果那個女子也愛那個男子，她就站在男子的前面，也用雙手去拉拉他的衣帶。這樣男子就知道她也愛着一他。於是他忙着去找一個可以去向女子一的父母說親的媒人。　　媒人一找到，男子的父母就帶了許多禮物和他一同到女子的家里去拜訪。媒人把男子的財產淸單拿出來給女子的父母看。他們考慮了一下，認為滿意，就當面答應了把他們的女兒嫁給那個男子。　　第二年，在那個大城市里又舉行市集，這對男女就在那里舉行了婚禮。在結婚的那一天，男女雙方都宰了幾只馴鹿，而新郎新娘還親自預備了筵席，欵待男女雙方的親戚。新郎更備了筵席欵待他的丈人丈母。婚禮舉行過之後，新娘就親手煮菜欵待全體來賓。　　還有一種特別的求婚方式。比仿一個男子愛上了一個女子。等有機會他就到女子的家去拜訪，帶着一只小碗，里面放着一克郎（一種瑞典銀幣—譯者）或兩克郎的錢幣，並且斟滿了白蘭地酒。他用了莊重而有禮的態度請那家的家長喝這碗酒。一看昆碗里放着錢幣，那位家長立刻知道來客的用意所在。假使他喝了那碗酒，這就表示他答應把他的女兒嫁給那個靑年了。（譯自世界語）藝壇評「無國遊民」  玲　　在過去許多美國底影片中，無論整部的，或者片段穿挿的，差不多都是披着人道主義色彩的外衣，而且還會出現過一些替黑人呌苦—母寗說是「可憐」—的片子，其中允以「黑奴籲天錄」一片給觀衆們底印象最深。　　但是，當你接受了每一個鏡頭之後，所能得到的不過是這些落後民族底「愚味」，「固執」，「野蠻」的暴露，幷且這都是在導演者們用主觀的支配，抓住了片段的特殊事賞加以强調後來完成的。可是，卽使在指明了這些受着自然條件限制所造成的弱點之後，他們也不過只是對這一事實發舒發舒自我的觀感而己，並不能更進一步地指示給我們，如何利用我們先進的良知來啟示他們，誘導他們，以改簪生活。有的，却是炫耀着如何利用科學方法和優良的物質條件，來統治他們，壓迫他們，直至他們心服口服而後已。例如最近在辣斐大戲院出演的「非洲戰爭」一片中，當着英國總督用機關槍鎮服了土人暴動之後，他對一個投降的酋長擺出勝利微笑的面孔說：「這就是大英帝國的神秘！」　　蘇聯底「無國游民」的演出，在這弱小民族簡直無法出氣的時代，當着用飛機大砲向這些被歧視的民族「宣揚文明」的時代，這意義是非常偉大的。但在「無國游民」一片中，如果說是對外的諷刺，莫如說是蘇聯的民族政策的自我說明，和民族政策實踐勝利的自詡。　　素材的內容是寫一羣失了國家，過着流浪游牧生活的吉普塞人，在一個狡猾的領袖統治之下，頑固地保持着無文字的法律，整年整月地住蒼無頂的房子，連快慰地休息一下都不能夠：蘇聯不忍看着這羣流浪人的非人性的生活，派了許多宣傳人員到吉普塞人的集團中去工作，勸誘他們放棄這種非人的流浪生活，加入到集體農村去，享一些人生的樂趣。我們知道吉普塞人是世界上一種「神秘」的民族，他們沒有國家和最高的文化做聯繫，但能流浪到歐洲各地保持着特殊的生活方式：吉香塞人具有火燄似的熱情，和藝術化的情感，對音樂更有特殊的天才，著名歌劇　Carman（卡門）就是寫流浪在西班牙的吉普塞姑娘的戀愛故事。但同時，因為他們沒有正當的生產和過蒼枯燥的單調生活，又把他們養成了頑强不化的個性，幷使他們營着一些不合法的犯罪生活。當宣傳員伊萬百般勸導他們到農村中去過安樂生活時，雖然得到了其中的靑年吉普塞人們底同情，但終因為達尼洛怕失去個人底領袖地位，不惜一再用陰謀手段從中挑撥起吉普塞人對集體農村的惡感。第一次在盛大的聯歡會中，他慫恿對集體農村較有信仰的允德歐的女兒阿麗打去偷村中底鷄，以便借機率領着這羣吉普塞人離開農村，仍去過那流浪生活，同時也可永久地保持着他那領袖的權威。但此種陰謀為集體農村底領袖所識破了，他對於偷鷄的事並不加注意，反而對吉普塞人更加親善起來。這樣，吉普塞人深受感動，都自願把馬借給集體農村去工作，而從前受伊萬影響最大的允德歐，目親集體農村農民有秩序的耕作生活和所享受的物質待遇——這裏有一望無涯的麥穗，有整潔的房屋，有鷄塲，有曳引機，有汽車—人類向上求生的心，受了這樣優美的環境的啟示，那能不有動於中呢？他被感動得將要流出淚來，便毅然決然地加入了集體農村；他認可依着吉普塞人的法律，獨自一個人拖着妻子女兒們走到集體農村去。尤德歐一個人拖着幾百斤重的車輛和人口，在泥淖的路上拚命地掙扎着，這完全是受了求生熱力的鼓勵的。當蒼集體農村開歡迎允德歐大會時，他們又把其他的吉普塞人都請來參加。陰險的達尼洛，因為領袖慾的燃燒，又想出了破壞集體農村和吉普塞人中間感情的陰謀來。他因為懷恨允德歐的投向農村，趁着大家在歡的時候，乘機把允德歐底女兒阿麗打刺死，當衆說是被農村領袖夫人因醋勁殺死的。於是達尼洛又率領着全體吉普塞人走去了。這樣直到阿麗打復蘇，詳述達尼洛陰謀後，全體吉普塞人才脫離了陰險的達尼洛，加入集體農村去了。　　素材的採取和組織，像似很平凡而又不甚統一。常着伊萬加入吉普塞人隊中去時，一點伏錢也沒有，使人感到了非常突然。在阿麗打轉着渡河的輪乘的幾個鏡頭，在導演者固然是有意地指出了這種不科學的方法是如何地費力而得不到效率，但接連就是三個同樣的鏡頭，不免有些單調和枯燥。其次，關於聯接方面，如伊萬領着普吉塞人到集體農村去，從中挿進了一農民晨間正在刷馬和他對着朝陽發牢騷的一個鏡頭，這像似離前面的節目太遠，使觀衆的情感突然隔開了主題。他如阿麗打和村中領袖夫人發生爭執，和夜間達尼洛訪村中領袖的一個鏡頭，也都犯了以上的毛病，如果能把這一段栽掉的話，我想常不致有傷於主題，因為此中的每一個特寫都可在另一個契機中表現出來的。　　「無國游民」在素材的處理方面固然有着這些缺點，但在劇情進展過程的每一個微小的製機中，却都能把每個角色底性格很深刻地描晝出來；而且每一個特性的描畫，雖然能夠給觀衆一個具體的輪廓和印象，但整個的片干裏却幷沒有一幕因此而對某一形象誇大的造作，像其他影片中一再地硬生生地挿人特寫，尤其是臉譜化的特寫。宣傳員伊萬能不避暴風　的襲擊，利用着這一機會勸導達尼洛到農村　，他能冒險去救允德歐以陳得吉普塞人的信仰；常着村中領袖不甚耐煩達尼洛的囉囌時候，他却發出了「吉普塞人到北冰洋去，我也追釗北冰洋」堅決的聲音；尤其是這一段—達尼洛檢了一些瘦羸不堪的老馬給村中送去了，一個農民有意地用手指撥着馬底脇骨，表示着嘲笑，伊萬制止他那浮躁的態度，說是不唯與事無濟，且恐惹起對方惡感：這一角色，都能在你不知不覺中，給你一個有理智，有熱情，有勇氣，沉着，負責任，有自信心的靑年典型。這可說純是導演者的力量。我國從事電影藝術的人們是應該學習的。他如達尼洛底陰險，允德歐底樸實，阿麗打底重情感，也都用同一的手法表達出來的。　　「無國游民」底第二個特點是理論的藝術化，它能把很深奧的理論用形象表達出來，而同時又含蒼說明意味。牠申述了世界上民族雜處的國家應當如何用平等待遇的態度，才能解決這一問題。吉普塞人投向集體嚴村，幷不是用機槍大炮的壓迫，和把哲理化為陰謀手段才能做到的。他們是用着百折不撓的說服精神和事實的教訓，才使這羣頑固不化的流浪者們心服了。　　樸實的允德歐為什麽對集體農村傾服了呢？這完全是因為伊萬底宣傳，但宣傳幷不是欺騙，況且同時又有鐵額事實證明。尤德歐在村中領袖親自教導鼓勵之下，學會了割麥子；勞作室人生底娛樂，所以他得到了從未得到過的快樂。他有工作同時就得到了房屋，得到了一切應得的物質，當他在返家途中引吭高歌着：「明年我就有牛了，牛還能產牛奶給我喝呵！」他那愉快的表情使觀衆都被他感動而流淚了。其决，「無國游民」指示給我們的是：「民族」這一意義是建築在組成這一民族的每個人的利害關係上的。為了個人底領袖慾和英雄主義而妨碍了大多數人利益的人，一定會遭到滅亡，而達尼洛就是在這樣的過程中被毀滅了。達尼洛為他個人底領袖地位，不惜出賣他本族底令譽，而指使阿麗打去偷鷄：再不惜刺死他底同族人，以假罪于他人；他因為個人底惡感，對允德歐的困累不惟毫無同情心，而且反阻止來扶助允德歐的同族人，甚至還阻止農民和伊萬底援助；達尼洛底自私，殘暴，這都是埋下了的他所以失敗的伏綫。　　最後，應當特別提及的是攝影的技巧，在晨陽，夕照和阿麗打河濱夜唱的幾張畫面裏，可說是盡了攝影技巧的能事。不過在挿人的技巧上略嫌生硬，有些破壞了劇情進展底連擊，比起「慾燄」畫面底柔和自然來，似較遜一籌。　　但，「無國游民」一片無疑地是一部成功的作品，是我們弱小民族底必需的讀物；我們能從這一影片中得到其他影片所沒有的東西。訓練與修養三「靠」  克勤　　我們中國，靠天吃飯的人很多。自然，我們這裏所說的靠天吃飯，幷不是說他們一事不做，而是說，他們做儘管做，而且「勤爬苦掙」地去做，但是他們認為做是一回事，做過後有不有結果，又是一同事。比如格言上「只問耕耘，不問收穫」兩句話，就表明了你只管努力做，不要去問收成，做了自然有酬報的。但是這樣的態度是不是對的呢？我們就以農村那種土式的養蠶法為例，他們一天從朝到晚都是辛辛苦苦地在養蠶，但是及到蠶見成熟正要吐絲織繭的時候，蠶兒忽然發生瘟疫，這時蠶娘們除了燃香點燭，求神保佑外，只有聽天由命。還有，他們認為天乾水旱也是上天降下的浩刦，用來處罰惡人的，所以終年勤勞，不得一飽，他們也不怨天允人，只認自己該受。於是做就只是做，不問為甚麽要做，不間怎樣做，不問做了的結果如何，好與不好，成與不成，只靠着天老爺，旁的沒有法子。　　還有一種人，他們根本就不做，只想得「橫財」，吃「嗟來之食」。他們事事都依靠人，自己一點責任也不負。而且有些人還聲聲口口說自己命運不好，說人家不大帮他的忙，因之他的事業沒有成就，前途沒有希望，然而自己却一點也不肯努力。　　上面這兩種人，一種是靠天主義，一種是靠人主義。如果我們只靠天，那麽不怕我們如何努力，而不目的意識性地去行動，只是自然生長性地去行動，其結果，是冤枉白費了許多人力，比如不學習新的蠶絲科，懂得蠶病之醫治法，則數十日之功便要廢於一朝；而且如不預為造林防旱，預為浚河防水，而只把天乾水旱歸諸命運，只知道水來了才去築堤，旱來了才去掘井，那還是沒有多大辦法的。還不說根本不做事而希望得天之報的靠天主義是空想，行不通，就是努力工作而不加以認識分析的靠天主義，也不免要白費許多心血，走許多轉路。所以靠天主義是要不得的，我們要努力，要勤苦，但是要有目的，要有計劃，要有認識。　　至於靠人主義呢？那更是笑話。人類原是社會的動物，一個社會，一個人羣之能存續下去，完全是要整個社會的成員通力合作，「集衆思，廣衆慮」，才能生存和進化。若果有一部份的食利者，寄生者，想把責任完全推到他人身上，把勞動的工作推到另一部分人去做，而自己則驕奢淫逸，養尊處優，那麽這個社會內部便顯然要分做兩種不同的人羣，就不免有爭鬥衝突之發生，因為那一個入不願意安逸舒適，而那一個人又願意勤苦勞動呢？所以就整個社會來說，靠人主義是行不通的。就個人說，我這一次靠人，難道下一次人家還不聰明，還要白白地帮我的忙不成？反過來說，我們又願不願意光是「為他人作嫁衣裳」，「捨己田而耘人之田」呢？進一步說，如果人人都依靠人，即是說人人都不作事，那誰又能依靠誰呢？所以根本要互助，要以自己之助人，換得人家之助我，這樣，個人也才能生活下去。　　以下接第六版

Japanese Withdrawal from Three Northeastern Provinces: Joint Meeting Held Yesterday, Discussion of Various Issues Regarding China, Hirota's Military Maneuver Visit Postponed, Kawagoe's Visit to Zhang Undecided, Fourth Meeting Expected Next Week 1

(Tokyo) Public sentiment in Japan, sparked by the killing of Japanese sailors in Hongkou, Shanghai, has calmed down. However, Prime Minister Hirota, recognizing the continuing severity of Sino-Japanese relations, has postponed his trip to Hokkaido to attend the army's grand maneuvers to September 30th. Leading figures from the Japanese Foreign, Army, and Navy ministries held an important meeting this afternoon to review the latest state of Sino-Japanese relations and discuss potential solutions to future incidents. Due to the Hokkaido maneuvers, the cabinet meeting will be postponed to October 10th. (Reuter, 26th)

(Tokyo) The Japanese Army, Navy, and Foreign ministries held a joint meeting today. Isogu, Director of the Military Affairs Bureau of the Army Ministry, Toyota, Director of the Military Affairs Bureau of the Navy Ministry, and Kuwashima, Director of the East Asia Bureau of the Foreign Ministry, attended. They discussed various important issues based on forecasts of extreme developments. It is rumored that Prime Minister Hirota, in light of the seriousness of the situation, has abandoned his plan to accompany and observe the grand maneuvers in Hokkaido. The Tokyo Metropolitan Police Department today issued orders to protect Chinese residents. (Central News Agency, 26th)

Discussion

Next Year's Japanese Budget 11

— Yi

Japan, for the sake of its military policy, is willing to take extreme risks in finance. This is most evident in the national budget.

Since Japan forcibly occupied our four northeastern provinces, national expenditures have expanded year after year due to the intensification of military expansion. They have had to continuously use the two methods of increasing taxes and issuing public bonds to make up for the deficit. The people's tax burden is now almost unbearable, and the total amount of national debt, according to the latest announcement by the Ministry of Finance, has also broken the record of 10 billion yen. However, next year's Japanese national budget still continues this risky trend.

According to a Reuters dispatch, next year's Japanese budget, although the Ministry of Finance has made routine reductions to the amounts requested by various ministries, the total amount will undoubtedly exceed 3 billion yen. Because, according to the figures submitted by the ministries, the total budget for next year will increase to 3.5 billion yen. It is unlikely that the Ministry of Finance will be able to deduct as much as 400 or 500 million yen.

The most prominent feature of this budget is the sharp increase in the expenses of the Army and Navy. The Army Ministry has decided to implement a new national defense plan, which will require 3 billion yen over six years, as requested by Army Minister Terauchi and approved by the Emperor. According to this plan, the Army Ministry recently submitted a request to the Ministry of Finance for an army budget of 822 million yen for next year. This is an increase of 314 million yen compared to this year's army budget. Among this huge new budget, in addition to 336 million yen for regular army expenses, 166 million yen is designated for military expenses in Manchuria, and 300 million yen is designated for the first year of implementation of the new national defense plan. The Navy Ministry has submitted a naval budget of 770.5 million yen for next year, of which 340 million yen is designated for the Navy's new plan. All of this is noteworthy. If we add up the new budgets for the Army and Navy, we can see that next year's Japanese military expenses will account for more than 47% of the entire national budget. This is a higher percentage than the Army and Navy expenses accounted for this year.

What method will Baba use to support the next year's financial budget, which cannot expand without limit? Of course, he can only come up with the two magic weapons of increasing taxes and issuing public bonds. On the 22nd of this month, he submitted the "record-breaking" tax system reorganization plan to the cabinet for approval. There are four types of new taxes to be added and fifteen types of old taxes to be increased. However, after the implementation of this reorganization plan, it is estimated that the national tax revenue will only increase by 20 million yen in the first year. As for issuing public bonds, according to the announcement by the Ministry of Finance, the total amount of national debt borne by Japan as of August of this year is 9.889 billion yen, and the first issue of deficit public bonds for this year, 350 million yen, has already begun. According to general observation, the national public bonds borne by the Japanese financial world have long reached the saturation point. To make up for the shortfalls in next year's budget, Baba continues to issue public bonds, but the amount certainly cannot be too large. However, Japan's national revenue is only 1.6 billion yen, of which half must be made up by increased taxes and deficit public bonds in next year's budget. Unless Baba decides to take an even more risky path, I am afraid this difficult situation cannot be overcome.

At the time when this new budget had just begun to take shape, very noticeable effects had already occurred within Japan. According to a Tokyo telegram, the Tokyo stock market has been falling across the board since the 22nd of this month. It seems predictable that there will be even greater changes in Japan's economic and political circles due to this new budget proposal.

20,000 Hand Grenades Discovered in Factory Outside Brussels, Along with Multiple Machine Guns 17

Brussels: The search for illegal weapons continues to yield surprising results. It is reported that as many as 20,000 hand grenades have been discovered in a certain factory on the outskirts of the capital. Multiple machine guns were also discovered in the basement of a merchant in Antwerp. The residence of a gunsmith in the same area was also searched because several machine guns found in Liège were marked as being received by the gunsmith. During a search of a factory in Tongres near Liège, it was discovered that someone had ordered 50,000 hand grenades from the factory, which is currently being secretly manufactured, with a daily output of 500. It is reported that the factory was searched after a document from a Spanish captain was found in a briefcase. The Brussels police searched a certain business, having heard that the business had received an order from a certain foreign country posing as Mexico, ordering 20,000 bombs. A batch of illegal weapons was recently found on a ship near the port of Ostend. The prosecutor in Brussels has ordered the arrest of six people related to the case, including two Socialist members of the Brussels City Council. (Reuter, 26th)

Collapse of the Franc Bloc, French Cabinet Decides, Gold Nationalized, Franc Devalued, Britain, America, and France Establish Currency Agreement, Belgium and Switzerland Join, Netherlands Remains Temporarily Watchful, International Financial Stability Expected 20

(Paris) The government has decided to devalue the franc and nationalize all gold. (Reuter, 26th)

(Paris) Britain, France, and the United States have established a currency agreement. The government issued a communique yesterday evening stating that Britain, France, and the United States have concluded a currency agreement, stipulating that the legal price of the franc is equivalent to nine-tenths of gold, i.e., between 0.049 grams and 0.043 grams (originally 0.0655 grams), so that the economic relations of these countries can be practically reorganized, thereby stabilizing currency parities. Other countries may also join this agreement in the future. At the same time, the Ministry of Finance issued an order to establish an equalization fund of 10,000,000,000,000 francs for the purpose of stabilizing the currency. (Havas, 26th)

(London) Switzerland and Belgium have decided to join the currency agreement between Britain, France, and the United States. This shows that Switzerland will also implement a devaluation of the Swiss franc. The details of Switzerland's currency devaluation are currently kept secret, but will be the same as France's. Although Belgium has joined the international currency agreement, it will maintain its already devalued currency. The Netherlands, in view of the large amount of gold currently flowing from the Netherlands to the United States, has repeatedly stated that it will maintain the gold standard. However, whether the Netherlands will also reorganize its currency along with other major countries has now become a question. The Dutch cabinet will meet on Sunday to discuss the overall situation. Dr. Trip, President of the Netherlands Bank, declared that the Netherlands is prepared to deal with the impact of the devaluation of the franc and therefore has no need to worry. At the same time, it is generally believed that if the Netherlands also devalues the guilder, then the time to convene an international monetary conference will be ripe. The Berlin financial community believes that Germany may devalue the mark later, while Italy does not seem to be taking any action at present. (Reuter, 26th)

Franc Devaluation by Approximately 30%; Parliament to Hold FierCE Debate Tomorrow 21

(Paris) The government resolved late last night to devalue the franc and nationalize all gold. The new franc's value will henceforth be between 43 and 49 out of 900 parts pure gold per 1,000 (one part per million per gram). The pound sterling will be valued between 96 and 103 francs. A stabilization fund of 1,000,000,000,000 francs will be established to maintain this new equilibrium. The government has ordered the stock exchange to temporarily suspend trading pending further instructions. Another decree stipulates that debtors may request a suspension of payments for all commercial gold or foreign currency obligations due after September 26th. To protect the interests of those who have fixed mortgage loans, government and municipal loans will be forcibly converted on a 5% basis. It is reported that the government has drafted 16 bills to implement the new financial plan, which will be submitted to Parliament. These include provisions to compensate French citizens who have suffered significant losses. The Chamber of Deputies, according to custom, is usually convened in November, but a special session has been scheduled for Monday to discuss financial matters. It is expected that the new composition of the franc can be approved before noon on Tuesday. Once the government's new procedures have been passed, Parliament will adjourn until October 27th. This financial debate is expected to be very intense, but Communist Party members are now increasingly inclined to support the devaluation of the franc. (Reuters, 26th)

(Paris) Following the establishment of the tripartite monetary agreement between Britain, France, and the United States, in addition to devaluing the franc, Finance Minister Auriol issued a circular stating that all commercial debts due after September 26th that must be repaid in gold or foreign currency should be temporarily suspended. Simultaneously, a bill was drafted proposing the nationalization of all gold to be submitted to Parliament for discussion. Furthermore, at the close of the stock exchange yesterday afternoon, securities trading was extremely active, with a surge in buyers. To prevent disturbances, the government decided that all buyers should trade in cash. It is expected that when Parliament holds an extraordinary session on Monday, members of all parties will fully support the various bills proposed by the government, including the Communist Party members. In addition, National Economy Minister Spinasse will fly to Basel, Switzerland, to meet with officials of the Bank for International Settlements. Financial experts will also hold talks with experts from the Netherlands and Switzerland. Observers believe that all these contacts aim to ensure that the guarantees provided by Britain and the United States to support France are also supported by other countries. According to reports from Switzerland, responsible officials there expect the government to follow the Netherlands' lead and decide to maintain the gold standard. (Havas, 26th)

(Paris) Significant changes to the French monetary system are imminent, and the currencies and exchange rates of Britain, the United States, and France will create a new situation, with a massive impact on the international economic and financial community. This afternoon, the French government convened a special cabinet meeting on this matter, which lasted for four hours, concluding at 8 PM. It was decided to convene an extraordinary session of Parliament on Monday to approve extremely important financial bills. The nature of these bills remains unclear. However, it is said that the governments of Britain, the United States, and France have been negotiating on monetary issues for three months, with absolute secrecy maintained, so almost no one outside knows about it. It is now reported that the tripartite government negotiations have made headway and that a communiqué will be issued simultaneously tonight in London, Washington, and Paris, announcing the tripartite monetary agreement between Britain, the United States, and France to stabilize world prices. The French government has convened Parliament in an emergency for this matter, and it is expected that Parliament will be able to vote on the various monetary bills before noon on Tuesday. Prime Minister Léon Blum, who was originally scheduled to depart for Geneva tonight, has postponed his trip. The Paris Stock Exchange has been ordered to close on Monday to avoid market turmoil. Trading on the exchange today remained very active, with firm prices and many French securities buyers, with almost all prices rising at the close. As for the so-called new monetary bills, the government's communiqué is extremely brief, making it impossible to discern their contents. However, it is generally understood that the government seems to have decided to change the exchange rate between the franc and the pound sterling to a ratio of one to one hundred (i.e., one pound is worth one hundred francs; according to the current exchange rate, one pound is worth about seventy-six francs). It is said that this exchange rate has been agreed upon with the governments of Britain and the United States and will be passed by the extraordinary session of Parliament on September 28th. In addition, there are bills on preventing the outflow of cash and implementing rules for the new monetary bills, totaling sixteen bills. As for the communiqué issued by the governments of Britain, the United States, and France in London, Washington, and Paris, it will have to wait until after midnight tonight to be announced. The Council of the Bank of France is currently meeting to discuss the impact of this new bill on the issuing system. French and foreign economists here all acknowledge that the new monetary bill will have a significant effect on promoting the recovery of the world's currency and economy. This bill, after being discussed at the extraordinary sessions of the Senate and the House of Representatives, should be passed on Monday or Tuesday. Subsequently, Parliament will adjourn until it reconvenes on October 27th. Some people are deeply concerned that the Communist Party's opposition to the devaluation policy will lead to opposition to the government's new bill in Parliament, but according to recent news, the Communist Party, in consideration of the current environment, will likely vote in favor of the government. (Havas, 25th)

(Paris) After the cabinet decided on various bills concerning the new monetary policy yesterday, Prime Minister Léon Blum, Finance Minister Auriol, National Economy Minister Spinasse, Interior Minister Salengro, and Deputy Director of the Treasury Equalization Fund Rueff held a meeting at the Prime Minister's Office at 11:45 AM today to study the reactions that this bill may cause. Except for a portion that will be incorporated into the 1937 fiscal budget, other bills, such as the nationalization of cash, the new exchange rate for the franc, relief for veterans, and relief for small bondholders of municipal public bonds, are scheduled to be submitted to Parliament for discussion on Monday. The Finance Committee of the Chamber of Deputies is scheduled to meet first at 2:30 PM tomorrow, at which time Finance Minister Auriol will explain the various bills. Prime Minister Léon Blum may also attend at the same time. (Havas, 26th)

(Paris) After the cabinet decided on the devaluation of the franc, it recently resolved on seven bills: (1) Nationalization of cash; (2) All spot and forward transactions in foreign currency executed between September 20th and 26th must be reported to the government; (3) Salaries and wages should be adjusted to correspond with the cost of living; (4) Small bondholders and holders of 1936 government treasury bills should be provided with relief; (5) The delegated law orders issued by the previous Laval cabinet regarding the reduction of veterans' benefits should be repealed; (6) Measures for the repayment of public bonds of local autonomous bodies; (7) The bill to reduce public bond interest by 10% and food import taxes should be repealed. In addition, the current import tax rates are also planned to be adjusted (Havas, 26th).

(Paris) The French franc monetary standard is about to undergo a major change. Here is a review of the history of the French monetary standard for the reference of the general public. According to the law promulgated on the 17th day of the 7th month of the 11th year of the French Republican Calendar (i.e., 1803), the franc was established as the monetary standard. This law has been in effect for over a hundred years without modification. It was only in August 1914, with the start of the Great War, that the government ordered the specification of the market price of the franc. When the monetary standard law was first promulgated, it was based on silver, with each franc equivalent to five grams of pure silver. In the mid-19th century, the franc gradually switched to the gold standard. Initially, the gold-silver ratio was set at 1:15.5. Subsequently, the free use of silver coins was restricted, and the franc became a fully gold-standard currency, with each franc equivalent to 0.322 grams of pure gold. This legal price was maintained until the new law was promulgated on June 25, 1928, when the legal price of the franc was changed to 0.0655 grams of 90% gold per franc. Article 4 of the 1928 law also stipulated that the gold reserves of the Bank of France should account for at least 35% of the total amount of circulating banknotes and deposits. (Havas, 25th)

The Gold Standard is Gone 22

(Tokyo) Since Britain and the United States abandoned the gold standard, France is now the only country still on the gold standard, together with the franc bloc of the Netherlands and Switzerland, maintaining a lone stronghold to this day. The franc has been in crisis frequently for three years, and France has made national efforts to maintain the gold standard. Since the outbreak of the Spanish Civil War, the European political situation has become unstable and has exposed the disunity of the People's Front cabinet, which has been exploited by speculators, and the outflow of gold has increased dramatically. Therefore, Prime Minister Blum has no choice but to lower the parity. According to the French government, the implementation of the suspension of convertibility undoubtedly means abandoning the gold standard. Although only the United States nominally maintains the gold standard, it is actually off the gold standard. Therefore, France's abandonment of the gold standard is the final step, and there are now no gold standard countries in the world. (Domei News Agency, 26th)

Britain, the United States, and France Simultaneously Issue Declarations: Maintain Exchange Rates and Promote Peace 23

(Paris) The tripartite financial agreement between Britain, the United States, and France was originally scheduled to be announced at 11 PM last night, but it was delayed slightly due to a setback. At 1 AM this morning, French Finance Minister Auriol telephoned the U.S. Treasury Department. France's move to lower the value of its currency is widely seen as a consequence of the tripartite financial agreement. There is no doubt that the French government's new monetary policy has the understanding of the British and American governments. It is now believed that the British and American governments will both guarantee that they will not raise the value of their currencies after the franc is devalued. Well-informed financial circles believe that France only wants to lower the value of the franc within the framework of the pound sterling and the U.S. dollar currency zones. These negotiations have been ongoing for the past three months. (Reuters, 26th)

(Paris) Regarding the tripartite monetary agreement between Britain, France, and the United States, French Finance Minister Auriol and National Economy Minister Spinasse jointly issued a statement saying, "Regarding monetary issues, we made some explanations to Parliament on June 16th of this year. We are well aware that, continuing in this way, our country will inevitably be forced to adopt a self-sufficient policy or implement unilateral currency devaluation, neither of which is the best strategy. Now, the three democratic countries of Britain, France, and the United States have concluded a monetary agreement, which should be supported by other countries, especially Belgium. The central banks of Britain, France, and the United States should also take joint action to supplement what is not covered in the agreement. As far as France is concerned, this move can expand the credit system, thereby making it easier to complete great social undertakings." (Havas, 26th)

(London) The Treasury announced today that the British government, after consulting with the governments of France and the United States, has decided to cooperate to affirm the common desires of those countries as follows: (1) To promote the various conditions that will help to maintain peace; (2) To ensure the restoration of international economic relations; (3) To adopt a policy that will promote world prosperity. The British government must give primary consideration to the needs of internal prosperity of the territories of the British Empire in its policy on international monetary relations. The governments of France and the United States, shall give it also, similar consideration, on a mutual basis. The British government further declares that it will continue to maintain the policies it has adopted in recent years, which has the general objective of maintaining the greatest possible equilibrium in the international exchange system and making every effort to avoid any disturbing movements in the British currency. The British government shares the view of the French and American governments that a continuation of such a double policy will enable the governments to achieve the common objectives they desire. It is reported that the French government has notified Britain that, given the need for stability of various major currencies, a permanent equilibrium must be achieved in the various economic systems before it can be obtained. Therefore, the French government has decided to submit to its parliament a bill to reorganize the French currency. The British and American governments welcome this decision by France and hope that it can establish the stability of international economic relations on a more solid foundation. The governments of Britain, France, and the United States now jointly declare that they intend to continue to use various sources to ensure that the results of the proposed reorganization do not cause any fundamental disruption to international exchange. The three governments further believe that the success of the aforementioned policy is closely related to the development of international trade and believe that immediate action should be taken to find ways to abolish the current system of price limits and exchange controls. With the consent of the United States and France, the British government intends to invite other countries to join the cooperation so that they can have a considerable understanding of the policies outlined in this communiqué. According to reports, the British communiqué is the result of discussions among the relevant parties over the past few days. France has hinted at the possibility of reorganizing the value of the franc. The discussions were limited to the three most important countries mentioned above because expanding the scope would not be in line with the principle of confidentiality. It is also reported that although Britain has issued a communiqué, there will be no changes to its monetary system. (Reuters, 26th)

(Washington) Treasury Secretary Morgenthau issued a statement today on the imminent devaluation of the franc, the content of which is identical to that issued by Britain. The statement stated that the Treasury Department will make every effort to avoid disturbing the international exchange basis after the franc is adjusted, and said that the Treasury Department will continue its policy of stabilizing exchange rates. Finally, it stated that this is a turning point for world peace. (Guomin News Agency, 25th)

(Washington) Albert, the financial counselor of the French Embassy in the United States, has repeatedly met with Lockhart, the director of the U.S. Treasury's Equalization Fund; Haas, the director of the Treasury's research; Oliphant, the Treasury's counselor; Fees, the State Department's financial expert; and Taylor, the Under Secretary of the Treasury. An agreement was reached today, which is a prelude to the adjustment of the franc. The content of the agreement is still strictly confidential, but it is reported that France hopes that the United States can guarantee that, in the event of a devaluation of the franc, the gold content of the U.S. dollar will not be further reduced. As for the pound sterling, it is reported that France has obtained the British government's promise. This agreement was actually agreed upon last night, and Britain will also join. Previously, the U.S. authorities were unwilling to provide a formal guarantee because they wanted to study the impact of the franc's devaluation on the pound sterling and world exchange rates. According to the Treasury authorities this morning, the United States may stop using the Equalization Fund and allow the franc to rise and fall on its own, which will force France to move towards devaluation, or it must follow in Britain's footsteps and implement a gold export ban and abandon the gold standard, or partially abandon the gold standard like Belgium. (Guomin News Agency, 22nd)

(New York) Regarding the tripartite monetary agreement between Britain, France, and the United States, after the financial counselor of the French Embassy, Abel, held all-day talks with U.S. Treasury Secretary Morgenthau yesterday, responsible officials recently declared that the purpose of the talks was to discuss how the United States' policy on gold exports should be necessarily amended, because according to this policy, gold exports should be limited to countries on the gold standard. In addition, U.S. Treasury Secretary Morgenthau also told reporters that the United States' original position on the monetary agreement has been fully protected. This agreement is a preliminary step towards consolidating world peace, which I have been hoping for for three years. As for the exchange rate between the U.S. dollar and the pound sterling, although there have been changes, they have been very slight. (Havas, 25th)

Chaotic Exchange Market 24

(London) Foreign exchange trading here has been suspended today, and there is no trading in gold, so no prices have been quoted. London is very surprised by the franc's devaluation. All markets are in disarray. Because there is no price for foreign exchange, the settlement price of goods has no basis to rely on. However, the Amsterdam exchange rate opened in the morning from 7.30 to 7.35, and the New York exchange rate was from 4.915 to 4.95. Foreign exchange experts all said that the instability of the market caused by the franc's devaluation will probably have to wait until the French Parliament passes the measures proposed by the cabinet before it can gradually calm down. Therefore, the suspension of foreign exchange trading seems likely to be extended. The general sentiment in the market is definitely in favor of the bullish side, for two reasons: (1) It is expected that the new exchange rate between the U.S. dollar and the pound sterling will make the pound sterling cheaper than before, which will result in higher British prices; (2) It is believed that the franc's devaluation will be a stimulant for world trade. It is believed that after the franc's devaluation, the French funds that have been overflowing recently will not be repatriated in large quantities, and the anxiety about the final composition of the franc may not be settled for a while, because Prime Minister Blum's proposal for the franc's devaluation ranges from 25.19% to 34.551%, with a huge difference between the two figures, and it is not known which point will be settled. (Reuters, 26th)

(Tokyo) As a result of France's reduction in the value of the franc, the exchange rate between the British pound and the U.S. dollar fell by three-sixteenths of three in one fell swoop on the 26th, becoming 5 yuan 2 cents. The exchange rate between the Japanese yen and the U.S. dollar also fell by 2 jiao 6 fen, becoming 29 yuan 2 jiao 6 fen. According to observations by the Japanese exchange banks, the drop in the exchange rate of the Japanese yen is unavoidable, and it is gradually softening under the influence of the exchange rate between the British pound and the U.S. dollar. The Japanese steel, copper materials, and sugar industries will be affected, but the overall industry will not be greatly affected. (Domei News Agency, 26th)

English Newspaper Commentary: Sino-Japanese Accidental Incidents, Re-Aggression of North China, Arouse Anti-Japanese Sentiment, Japanese Must Consider Carefully Even if They Want War (London) Today's Meng Que Si Te Zhi Dao Bao reports that although the recent series of accidental incidents in China are unfortunate, all of them are the result of the spontaneous outburst of anti-Japanese sentiment among the Chinese people, and there is no official involvement, which is quite obvious. The world should pay more attention to the fact that although the Chinese government failed to prevent these incidents from happening, it immediately took swift and forceful measures afterwards to suppress the riots and severely punish the culprits. The newspaper then recalled the situation of the anti-Japanese sentiment that erupted after Japan's re-aggression of North China in October last year and expressed its opinion that Japan is probably only threatening the Chinese government and can no longer achieve its desire to continue to expand its power, because Nanjing will no longer make concessions because of threats. However, if the Chinese authorities cannot show submission to Japan, there is a serious danger that Japan will replay the events of the January 28th Incident in 1932, because the Japanese in Shanghai have long had the ambition to divide a part of the Chinese territory into a Japanese concession or to occupy Hongkou as their own. The Japanese have already secretly deployed their potential forces within the scope of the Shanghai Public Concession. Even worse, the Japanese military may repeat its old trick of separating the five provinces of North China to continue the unfinished business of Doihara Kenji, because the Japanese fear that Chairman Chiang Kai-shek has now placed the southwest under the central government's jurisdiction, or even attempt to restore the semi-autonomous sovereignty of North China. China is now nationally unified and has complete armaments, and its people's patriotic psychology is extremely enthusiastic. Even if Japan intends to go to war with China, it must consider it carefully, because it is not as easy as before. (Reuters dispatch on the 25th)

(Washington) Officials today hope that the recent incident in Shanghai can be resolved immediately without causing other disputes to disrupt the eventful Far East and international situation. This statement is based on the fact that the attitude of the Japanese naval authorities in Shanghai is more moderate than in 1932. It is said that Japan will put forward some new demands to China, and representatives of China and Japan will negotiate at length. As for the American troops stationed in Shanghai, they have been ordered to "remain in barracks on standby," but this is only a precautionary measure and does not mean that an incident is about to occur. Accused Investigator Assaults Someone, Wang Zhongfa Detained, Admits Theft, Why Released? Yang Yun Pays Compensation, Did Not Hit Him

A resident of No. 49, Avenue Orloff, French Concession, Zhenjiang native Yang Binglan, a leather craftsman, rented out the remaining pavilion room to Yan Renfa on the 13th of this month, stating that the monthly rent was five yuan. However, Yan moved in for seven days and still did not pay the rent. On the 22nd, at 4:00 PM, Yan suddenly claimed that five yuan in cash was stolen by Wu Xiaogouzi (14 years old, Danyang native), the apprentice of Yang Binglan, the second landlord. He reported this to the French Concession police. Investigator Wang Zhongfa went to investigate and detained Yang and his apprentice Wu Xiaogouzi, bringing them to the police station for questioning. After they were released at 9:00 PM that night, Yang and Wu, master and apprentice, claimed to have been assaulted and injured, and went to the hospital for treatment. After returning home, Wu Xiaogouzi still had alternating chills and fever, his whole body was swollen, and he was mentally disoriented. Yang informed Wu's father, Wu Jiangbei, who reported it to the police station. Yan Renfa, the plaintiff, was arrested on suspicion of false accusation and ordered to be detained. Wu Xiaogouzi was sent to the hospital for treatment. Wu Jiangbei also hired a lawyer and filed a lawsuit with the Special District Court for examination of injuries, as previously reported in this newspaper. It is now known that Yan Renfa has been escorted to the Special District Court by the police station, requesting detention for investigation, with a hearing postponed until the 28th (tomorrow morning). Yesterday, the police station also brought the investigator in charge, Wang Zhongfa, to the Special District Court. At noon, Judge Zhang Minsheng presided over the interrogation in the Eighth Criminal Court. Wang testified that he was 43 years old, from Tianjin. After Yan Renfa reported the case to the police station, he was sent to investigate and brought Yang Binglan and Wu Xiaogouzi to the police station. Wu Xiaogouzi admitted to stealing five yuan in cash. He was asked why Wu was released if he admitted to theft, and whether he had beaten them. He replied that Wu admitted to stealing and his master Yang Binglan agreed to pay compensation, so the police station released them and did not beat them. The court reviewed the testimony and adjourned the hearing to the 28th. Wang was detained.

The Bandit Who Shot and Killed a Policeman Was Arrested in Kunshan, Wang Er Directly Confesses 29

On the 31st of last month, at approximately 8:00 PM, Suzhou native Lin Weixue (21 years old), a policeman from the Caojiadu Public Security Bureau in western Shanghai, was on duty at post number two in front of the dormitory of the Central Geological Research Institute on Jessfield Road when he was attacked by four armed bandits. On the 17th, he fled to Kunshan. The suspect was immediately brought to Shanghai (the Mauser pistol remains in the Kunshan County Public Security Bureau). After interrogation by the detective squad leader, Wang confessed to having three accomplices and directly admitted to shooting and killing the policeman. The suspect was first transferred to the branch bureau for processing and will be sent to the headquarters.

Using Counterfeit Money for Postal Remittance, Suspicion Leads to Accusation, Yu Qimin States His Case, Ordered to Post 3,000 Yuan Bail

Yu Qimin, a 24-year-old from Yangzhou, went to the Kai Zi Tong Road postal branch at the west end of the French Concession's Ba Xian Qiao on the 25th at around 11:00 AM to send a ten-yuan money order to Lu Jiajun at the Kaiming Printing House on South Main Street in Funing County. On the front of the letter, he wrote that it was sent by Yuan Rongshu from No. 86 Xinqiao Street. He paid with one five-yuan banknote and five one-yuan banknotes from the China Farmers Bank. The postal clerk discovered that the five one-yuan banknotes were all counterfeit. The detective stationed at the bureau questioned Yu, who gave evasive answers. A search of his person uncovered over twenty yuan in real money. Yu was suspected of knowingly using counterfeit money and was taken to the French Concession police station and detained. Yesterday, he was escorted to the First Criminal Court of the Special District Court. Gu Shouxi, a lawyer from the police affairs department, stated the facts of the case, requested a postponement for further investigation, and then another hearing. The detective reported the details of the incident and submitted the counterfeit money as evidence. Yu testified that on the 24th, he traveled from the countryside of Yangzhou to Zhenjiang, took a night train to Shanghai to purchase engagement fabrics. He arrived in Shanghai yesterday morning and looked for his friend Yuan Rongshu but could not find him. He planned to stay at a hotel but remembered that his friend Lu Jiajun from Funing had written to him asking to borrow twenty yuan, so he went to the post office to remit ten yuan first. Because he had no address, he used Yuan's name, without knowing his address, and just randomly wrote the house number 86 Xinqiao Street. He really did not know that the banknotes were fake, and if he had known, he would never have used the five-yuan note together. Judge Wang Gangxu reviewed the testimony and ordered Yu to provide a 3,000 yuan shop guarantee. Without a guarantee, he would be detained and another hearing would be held on the 30th.

Muxin Hospital Opened Yesterday, Founded by Business Tycoon Lu Bohong, Wu Tiecheng Represented at the Unveiling

Yesterday at 3:00 PM, the Muxin Hospital in Zhabei held its opening ceremony. A reporter from the Huadong News Agency went to visit and report the details as follows:

Purpose of Founding

Lu Bohong, a tycoon in the industrial and charitable circles of this city, observed that the Zhabei area is vast and densely populated, especially with many laborers. The number of hospitals in the area is insufficient. He specially borrowed over 30 mu of land from the Xinpu'an Tang to build the Muxin Hospital to benefit the poor.

Group Photo of Guests at Muxin Hospital (International News Agency Photograph)

Number of Guests

The hospital invited guests from all walks of life to attend the ceremony. Those present included: Li Dachao, representative of the Municipal Government; Zhang Binghui, representative of the Social Affairs Bureau; Wang Binyan, Zhou Wenyuan, Zhu Kaichou, Xia Zanbo, Zhu Shaoqi, He Gangli, Wang Yiquan, Zhou Ren, Shen Shida, Zhu Zuoting, Xu Mufan, Liang Kezhong, Pan Wenfan, Yin Cunfu, Li Boji, Bei Yisun, Zhang Yipeng, Zheng Yucheng, Wang Zhiwei, Liu Hanru, Yuan Junchang, Shen Mingpan, Zhu Zhiyao, Xu Xinliu, Dong Junfu, Gong Qinyuan, Zhou Shanbin, Xu Dongren, Chen Chenchuan, Lu Honggao, and other Chinese and French guests, totaling four to five hundred people.

Construction Expenses

When Mr. Lu celebrated his sixtieth birthday the year before last, the birthday gifts from relatives and friends amounted to no less than thirty to forty thousand yuan. The current construction cost is nearly eighty thousand yuan. The shortfall was raised by Mr. Lu through fundraising. After two years of painstaking preparation, today's success was achieved.

Hospital Equipment

The hospital has three Western-style buildings (all eight stories high), and a statue of the Holy Mother is built at the front entrance. The front building is a male ward, the second building is a female ward, and the last building is a school building for a complete primary school (expected to open at the end of this year). The equipment is thorough and the air is fresh. Treatment for the poor is completely free. Mr. Lu serves as the hospital director (he graduated from the Faculty of Law at Aurora University and has a doctorate in law. He is currently the director of the Technical Section of the Zhabei Water and Electricity Plant Company). The doctors are Zeng Xianming and Song Wusheng. Four nurses who graduated from the French Royal Hospital are also employed.

Temporary Expenses

The hospital's estimated monthly expenses are between 1,500 and 2,000 yuan. In addition to the 500 yuan monthly grant from the Municipal Government, the remainder is the responsibility of the hospital director and philanthropist Shi Shengzhi.

Director's Report

The opening ceremony began at 3:00 PM. After Li Dachao, representing Mayor Wu Tiecheng, cut the ribbon, the guests entered the hall in succession. Lu reported, briefly stating that there were many laborers in the Zhabei area, and although there were several hospitals, they were not enough. If they fell ill, the expenses would be very high, and many would not be able to afford them. Therefore, there was a need to build a hospital for the poor. He specially allocated his birthday gifts from the year before last to be used for construction expenses to benefit the poor and sick.

Representative's Speech

Li Dachao, the representative of the Municipal Government, then delivered a speech, briefly stating that today was the ceremony for the opening of Muxin Hospital, founded by Mr. Lu Bohong. He was very honored to participate in the grand ceremony on behalf of the Municipal Government. Mr. Lu was charitable and enthusiastic about public welfare throughout his life. There are many poor people and few hospitals in the Zhabei area. Therefore, Mr. Lu thought about the poor and designed for the sick. Two years ago, he completely allocated his sixtieth birthday celebration gifts as the funds for today's successful Muxin Hospital, benefiting the poor in Zhabei. This was truly extraordinary. The guests were then invited by Director Lu to enjoy refreshments and have their photographs taken. At around 5:00 PM, everyone dispersed happily.

Two Taiwanese Counterfeit US Dollar Bills, Arrested at the Dadong Hotel

The Shanghai Times reported that the Special Criminal Division of the Public Works Department Police received a warning from the US authorities several days ago that someone was using counterfeit twenty-dollar bills in Shanghai and requested surveillance and investigation. Therefore, they immediately engaged in detective work. They learned that the perpetrators using the counterfeit bills were two Taiwanese men staying at the Dadong Hotel. Yesterday (the 25th), a Chinese detective was sent to Room 27 of the hotel on Nanjing Road to visit the two suspects, pretending to want to buy counterfeit bills. The two suspects believed him and closed the door to discuss the price, which was eight Chinese dollars per bill. The detective then offered a past-due check for less than three thousand yuan as payment. When the two suspects accepted the check and took out the counterfeit bills, the detective signaled, and the Western detectives waiting outside the door rushed into the room, arrested the two suspects, and seized 365 counterfeit bills, totaling 7,300 US dollars, equivalent to 24,000 Chinese dollars. The printing was very exquisite, revealing the work of an expert. Non-experts could not distinguish the forgery. Because the two suspects were Taiwanese, they have been transferred to the Japanese Consulate in Shanghai, and all information obtained has been handed over to the consulate. It is said that the consulate will continue to investigate thoroughly.

At around 10:00 PM the night before last, a young man around twenty years old, well-dressed, came to the Dahao Hotel at the Dongxinqiao intersection of Avenue Edward VII in the French Concession, accompanied by a modern woman. Commercial News & Finance Foreign News: Franc Devaluation Resolved, Gold Prices Soar; Major Speculators Vigorously Cover Short Positions, Penetrating the $40 Mark; Result: A Surge of $14.20

Yesterday's gold market saw a significant contraction in exchange rates, a sudden surge in raw gold prices, and a Reuters report that the French government had decided to devalue the franc. The hope of short sellers was realized, and buying interest intensified. In the early morning, overseas silver markets saw the British pound rise and the U.S. dollar remain flat. After the close, large traders adjusted their positions and quoted 0.0625. American speculators bought, while sellers remained on the sidelines. Montreal's forward silver prices remained unchanged, with discounts of 2.5% and premiums of 5% depending on the term. Exchange rates suddenly plummeted, and London's raw gold prices surged by 6.5 pence. The Central Bank's official exchange rates showed both the British pound and U.S. dollar unchanged, while customs gold units rose by 8 li. The standard gold price rose to $1120.50. Off-exchange preparatory trading opened weakly at $28. Due to the exchange rate collapse, it seemed that Britain and the United States were supporting the franc, and the trend for pure gold should rebound favorably. De Mao, Yong Sheng, Rui Xing, Qia Feng, and Yong Ju all advanced, nearly approaching the $39 mark. Heng Yu, Yuan Mao, Yong Da, and Heng divested, retreating to $8.34. The morning opened high and immediately rose, largely because the exchange market tightened and penetrated the $30 mark. HSBC's exchange rates showed the British pound flat and the U.S. dollar down 0.25, with the silver equalization tax rising by half a cent. There was some struggle mid-session, but then news came that the French government had decided to devalue the franc and would no longer raise its value. Generally, short sellers, their hopes realized, scrambled to cover. Even though major long players emerged in the market, the massive shorts from Tong Feng Heng and others vigorously covered, invigorating buying. Some long players seized the opportunity to increase their positions, driving prices above $40. Uninformed long positions emerged continuously. Prices briefly fell back after reaching a high, but ultimately remained above $40. Here is a record of the market conditions for half a day.

The morning opening was $1128.40, up $1.90 from the previous close. Yuan Chang, Yong Fu, Xing Yong, Yuan Mao, and Yong immediately advanced to $30. Da De Cheng and Heng Yu sold at $28.70. Folklore: No Pimping, Just Tug at the Sash; A Lifetime Commitment with One Cup of Coffee: The Unique Marriage System of the Sami People Zhang Qicheng

The Sami people (Laponoj) are a nomadic people living in northern Sweden, with a population of only seven thousand. Their language and lifestyle are very special, but what we find most special is their marriage system. They still practice a kind of arranged marriage. Here, we will discuss their arranged marriage system:

In Sami society, the customs of how a young man finds a wife are varied and quite interesting. The most common way is when a Sami boy grows into a young man and needs a woman, he must first find a matchmaker who can negotiate with the parents of the woman he loves. The first step is for him and his matchmaker to visit the girl's tent (because the Sami people all live in tents). Upon entering the tent, after exchanging greetings with the host, they sit quietly without saying a word for a while. Then, the young man, according to the pre-arranged plan, gives a signal to the matchmaker, who then begins to say: "May we brew some coffee here?" "Yes, yes, of course you may. Everyone has the right to brew coffee here." At this time, the Sami young man takes out the coffee pot and cups from his bag, fills the pot with clean snow (where there is snow all year round), and then puts it on the fire. As the water boils, the host and guests engage in idle chatter, but never mention the matter of marriage. While talking, the young man takes out sugar, dried cheese, and bread from his bag. Once the coffee is brewed, the young man drinks a cup himself, and then offers it to the male and female hosts. If the male and female hosts accept his coffee, it means that they understand the intention and fully agree to the marriage proposal. At this point, the young man can further ask their daughter to drink coffee with their consent. If the girl accepts the cup of coffee from the young man, it means that she also loves him. Then, both parties can go to the nearby registry to register their engagement, and finally, a pastor completes the wedding ceremony.

There are also young men who do not go to the girl's home themselves, but only send their matchmaker. The matchmaker goes to inquire if the girl's family has any objections to the marriage proposal. As a rule, the girl's parents will inquire about the man's property, asking how many reindeer he has (because reindeer can be said to be the Sami people's only property), and also inquire about his character. If the matchmaker's answers satisfy them, they can start the engagement banquet in the girl's tent. The future groom and the relatives and friends of both parties attend the banquet, and each relative and friend must bring some items (sometimes even very valuable things) as gifts for the engaged couple.

There are also men who first court the woman, and after the woman agrees, they ask a matchmaker to propose marriage. Once, in a market in a large city, a man bumped into a woman he loved. After they met, the man tugged at the woman's sash. This is the first sign of courtship. If the woman also loves the man, she stands in front of the man and also uses both hands to tug at his sash. This way, the man knows that she also loves him. So he hurries to find a matchmaker who can propose marriage to the woman's parents.

Once the matchmaker is found, the man's parents take many gifts and go with him to visit the woman's home. The matchmaker takes out the list of the man's property to show to the woman's parents. They consider it and are satisfied, so they agree to marry their daughter to the man in person.

The following year, the market was held again in that big city, and the couple held their wedding there. On the wedding day, both parties slaughtered several reindeer, and the bride and groom personally prepared a feast to entertain the relatives of both parties. The groom also prepared a feast to entertain his parents-in-law. After the wedding ceremony, the bride personally cooked dishes to entertain all the guests.

There is also a special way of proposing marriage. For example, a man falls in love with a woman. When he has the opportunity, he visits the woman's home, bringing a small bowl filled with one or two kronor (a type of Swedish silver coin—translator) and filled with brandy. He uses a solemn and polite manner to invite the head of the family to drink this bowl of wine. As soon as the head of the family sees the coins in the bowl, he immediately knows the intention of the visitor. If he drinks the bowl of wine, it means that he agrees to marry his daughter to the young man. (Translated from Esperanto)

Art Review: "Wandering Nomads" Ling 31

In many American films in the past, whether whole or in interspersed fragments, almost all of them are cloaked in the guise of humanitarianism, and there have even been some films that cry out for the suffering of black people—Mother Ning called them "pitiful"—among which the film "Uncle Tom's Cabin" gave the audience the deepest impression.

However, after you accept each shot, all you can get is the exposure of the "ignorance," "stubbornness," and "barbarism" of these backward ethnic groups, and this is all completed after the directors used subjective dominance to seize fragmentary special events and emphasize them. However, even after pointing out these weaknesses caused by the limitations of natural conditions, they only express their own feelings about this fact, and cannot further instruct us on how to use our advanced conscience to enlighten them, guide them, and improve their lives. What they do is flaunt how to use scientific methods and excellent material conditions to rule them, oppress them, until they are convinced. For example, in the recent film "African War" shown at the Lafayette Grand Theatre, after the British Governor used machine guns to suppress the native rebellion, he showed a victorious smiling face to a surrendered chief and said, "This is the mystery of the British Empire!"

The performance of the Soviet Union's "Wandering Nomads" is of great significance in this era when weak ethnic groups have no way to vent their anger, and when airplanes and cannons are used to "promote civilization" to these discriminated ethnic groups. However, in the film "Wandering Nomads," if it is said to be satire to the outside world, it is better to say that it is the Soviet Union's self-explanation of its ethnic policies, and the boasting of the victory of the practice of ethnic policies.

The content of the material is about a group of Gypsies who have lost their country and live a wandering nomadic life. Under the rule of a cunning leader, they stubbornly maintain unwritten laws, living in roofless houses all year round, unable even to rest comfortably. The Soviet Union could not bear to watch this group of wanderers live an inhuman life, and sent many propagandists to work in the Gypsy groups, persuading them to abandon this inhuman wandering life, join collective farms, and enjoy some of the pleasures of life. We know that Gypsies are a "mysterious" ethnic group in the world. They have no country or highest culture to connect them, but they can wander to various parts of Europe and maintain a special way of life. Gypsies have fiery enthusiasm and artistic emotions, and have a special talent for music. The famous opera "Carmen" is about the love story of a Gypsy girl wandering in Spain. But at the same time, because they have no proper production and live a monotonous life, they have developed a stubborn personality and engage in some illegal criminal activities. When propagandist Ivan tried his best to persuade them to go to the countryside to live a comfortable life, although he gained the sympathy of the young Gypsies, Danilo, fearing the loss of his personal leadership position, repeatedly used conspiracies to provoke the Gypsies' resentment towards collective farms. The first time, at a grand celebration, he encouraged Yudeou's daughter, Alida, who had more faith in collective farms, to steal chickens from the village, so as to take the opportunity to lead this group of Gypsies away from the farm and continue their wandering life, while also permanently maintaining his authority as leader. However, this conspiracy was seen through by the leader of the collective farm. He did not pay attention to the theft of chickens, but instead became more friendly to the Gypsies. In this way, the Gypsies were deeply moved and voluntarily lent their horses to the collective farm to work. Yudeou, who was most influenced by Ivan before, personally witnessed the orderly farming life of the collective farm farmers and the material treatment they enjoyed—here are endless fields of wheat, neat houses, chicken farms, tractors, and cars—the human heart's desire to live upwards, inspired by such a beautiful environment, how can it not be moved? He was so moved that he was about to shed tears, and resolutely joined the collective farm. He recognized that according to Gypsy law, he dragged his wife and daughters to the collective farm alone. Yudeou struggled desperately on the muddy road, dragging hundreds of pounds of vehicles and people alone, which was entirely encouraged by the heat of survival. When the collective farm held a welcome meeting for Yudeou, they also invited other Gypsies to participate. The insidious Danilo, burning with a desire for leadership, came up with a conspiracy to destroy the relationship between the collective farm and the Gypsies. Because he resented Yudeou's joining the farm, he took the opportunity to stab Yudeou's daughter, Alida, to death while everyone was celebrating, and publicly said that it was killed by the village leader's wife out of jealousy. So Danilo led all the Gypsies away again. This continued until Alida recovered and detailed Danilo's conspiracy, and all the Gypsies broke away from the insidious Danilo and joined the collective farm.

The selection and organization of the material seem very ordinary and not very unified. When Ivan joined the Gypsy team, he did not have any foreshadowing, which made people feel very sudden. In the several shots of Alida turning the ferry wheel to cross the river, the director intentionally pointed out how laborious and inefficient this unscientific method is, but there are three consecutive shots of the same scene, which is inevitably somewhat monotonous and dry. Secondly, regarding the connection, such as Ivan leading the Pujisai people to the collective farm, and inserting a shot of a farmer brushing a horse in the morning and complaining to the morning sun, this seems too far from the previous program, and suddenly separates the audience's emotions from the theme. Similarly, the scene where Alida has a dispute with the village leader's wife, and the scene where Danilo visits the village leader at night, also have the above problems. If this section can be cut off, I think it will not harm the theme, because each of these close-ups can be expressed in another opportunity.

Although "Wandering Nomads" has these shortcomings in the handling of materials, in every small opportunity in the progress of the plot, it can deeply portray the personality of each character; and although each characteristic depiction can give the audience a concrete outline and impression, the entire film does not have a single scene that exaggerates a certain image, like other films that repeatedly and forcibly insert close-ups, especially stereotyped close-ups. Propagandist Ivan can not avoid the attack of the storm and use this opportunity to persuade Danilo to go to the countryside, he can risk his life to save Yudeou in order to Chen get the Gypsy's faith; when the village leader is impatient with Danilo's nagging, he issues a firm voice saying "If the Gypsies go to the Arctic Ocean, I will chase to the Arctic Ocean"; especially this section—Danilo sent some thin and weak old horses to the village, a farmer intentionally flicked the horse's ribs with his fingers, expressing ridicule, Ivan stopped his impetuous attitude, saying that it would not only be of no help, but also would cause the other party's disgust: this role can give you a youth archetype with reason, enthusiasm, courage, composure, responsibility, and confidence without you realizing it. This can be said to be purely the power of the director. Our country's people engaged in film art should learn from it. Similarly, Danilo's insidiousness, Yudeou's simplicity, and Alida's emphasis on emotions are also expressed in the same way.

The second characteristic of "Wandering Nomads" is the artification of theory, it can express very profound theories with images, and at the same time contain explanatory meaning. It states how countries with mixed nationalities in the world should use equal treatment to solve this problem. The Gypsies' joining the collective village was not achieved by the oppression of machine guns and cannons, and by turning philosophy into conspiracy. They used an indomitable spirit of persuasion and the lessons of facts to convince this group of stubborn wanderers.

Why did the simple Yudeou admire the collective farm? This is entirely because of Ivan's propaganda, but the propaganda is not deception, and at the same time, there are ironclad facts to prove it. Yudeou learned to harvest wheat under the personal teaching and encouragement of the village leader; labor is the entertainment of life, so he got the joy he had never gotten before. He has work and at the same time gets houses and everything he deserves. When he sings loudly on the way home: "Next year I will have a cow, and the cow can produce milk for me to drink!" His happy expression moved the audience to tears. In short, what "Wandering Nomads" tells us is: the meaning of "nation" is built on the interests of each person who makes up this nation. People who hinder the interests of the majority for the sake of personal leadership desire and heroism will surely be destroyed, and Danilo was destroyed in this process. For his personal leadership position, Danilo did not hesitate to sell his clan's reputation, and instructed Alida to steal chickens; he did not hesitate to stab his clansman to death, and falsely accuse others; because of his personal resentment, he not only had no sympathy for Yudeou's distress, but also prevented his clansmen from helping Yudeou, and even prevented the farmers and Ivan's assistance; Danilo's selfishness and brutality were all buried in his failure.

Finally, it should be specially mentioned that the photography skills, in the several screens of morning sun, evening glow, and Alida's riverside night singing, can be said to have exhausted the capabilities of photography skills. However, the insertion skills are slightly stiff, and some of them destroy the continuity of the plot progress. Compared with the soft and natural "Desire Flame" screens, it seems slightly inferior.

However, "Wandering Nomads" is undoubtedly a successful work, and it is a necessary reading for our weak ethnic groups; we can get something from this film that other films do not have.

Training and Cultivation: Three "Rely" Keqin

In our China, there are many people who rely on heaven for food. Of course, what we mean by relying on heaven for food here is not that they do nothing, but that they do their best, and do it "diligently," but they believe that doing is one thing, and whether there are results after doing it is another thing. For example, the two sentences in the motto "Only ask about cultivation, not about harvest" show that you only need to work hard, don't ask about the harvest, and there will be rewards for doing it. But is this attitude correct? Let's take the rural earth-style sericulture method as an example. They work hard all day long from morning to night raising silkworms, but when the silkworms are about to mature and spin cocoons, the silkworms suddenly get sick. At this time, the silkworm mothers have no choice but to burn incense, light candles, and pray for God's blessing, but to listen to fate. Also, they believe that droughts and floods are also a catastrophe sent down by God to punish evil people, so they work hard all year round and cannot get enough to eat. They do not blame heaven or others, and only recognize that they deserve it. So doing is just doing, not asking why to do it, not asking how to do it, not asking what the results of doing it are, good or bad, successful or not, only relying on God, and there is no other way.

There is also a kind of people who do not do anything at all, but only want to get "windfall wealth" and eat "charity food." They rely on others for everything and do not take any responsibility themselves. And some people even say that they have bad luck, that others do not help them much, so their careers have not been successful and their future has no hope, but they themselves are not willing to work hard at all.

The above two kinds of people, one is the doctrine of relying on heaven, and the other is the doctrine of relying on others. If we only rely on heaven, then no matter how hard we work, and do not act with a sense of purpose, but only act with natural growth, the result is that a lot of manpower is wasted in vain. For example, if we do not learn new sericulture sciences and understand the treatment of silkworm diseases, then the work of dozens of days will be wasted in one morning; and if we do not build forests in advance to prevent drought, and do not dredge rivers in advance to prevent floods, but only attribute droughts and floods to fate, and only know to build dikes when the water comes, and only know to dig wells when the drought comes, then there is still not much way. Not to mention that the doctrine of relying on heaven, which does not do anything at all and hopes to get the reward of heaven, is a fantasy and does not work, even the doctrine of relying on heaven, which works hard but does not recognize and analyze, will inevitably waste a lot of effort and take many detours. So the doctrine of relying on heaven is unacceptable. We must work hard, we must be diligent, but we must have purpose, we must have plans, and we must have knowledge.

As for the doctrine of relying on others? That is even more ridiculous. Humans are originally social animals, and the survival and evolution of a society and a group of people completely depends on the cooperation of all members of the society, "collecting the thoughts of the people and considering the worries of the people widely," in order to survive and evolve. If there are some profiteers and parasites who want to push the responsibility entirely to others, and push the work of labor to another part of the people, while they themselves are extravagant and indulgent, and live in luxury, then this society will obviously be divided into two different groups of people, and there will inevitably be struggles and conflicts, because which one is not willing to be comfortable and which one is willing to work hard? So, for the whole society, the doctrine of relying on others does not work. In terms of the individual, if I rely on others this time, will people not be smart next time and still help me for nothing? Conversely, are we willing to "make wedding clothes for others" and "abandon our own fields to cultivate others' fields"? Furthermore, if everyone relies on others, that is, everyone does nothing, then who can rely on whom? Therefore, it is fundamental to help each other, to exchange our help to others for their help to us, so that individuals can live on.
